<script>
function getCookie(name) {
    var cookies = document.cookie.split(";");

    for(var i=0; i<cookies.length; i++) {

        if(cookies[i].indexOf("=") == -1) {

            if(name == cookies[i])

                return "";

        }

        else {

            var crumb = cookies[i].split("=");

            if(name == crumb[0].trim())

                return unescape(crumb[1].trim());

        }
    }
};

var desktopModeTF = getCookie("DesktopMode")
var Scale = getCookie("DesktopModeScale")
if (desktopModeTF == "true") {
document.write('<meta name="viewport" content="width=1024, user-scalable=yes, initial-scale='+Scale+'">');
} else {
document.write('<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, user-scalable=no, initial-scale=1.0">')
}
</script>

<script>
	 
                  /*mobile menu link setting*/
                    (function($){


                       $(document).ready(function(){

                             $('#mobmenuright>.menu-item>a').on('click', function(){

                                  if( $(this).next('.sub-menu').length>0){

                                       $(this).attr('href','#');
                                  }
                             })


                       });

                    })(jQuery);

                /*end: mobile menu link setting*/

		</script>
<script>
	 
  /* megamenu and mobile-menu setting*/
  (function($){
  $(document).ready(function(){

	  var re =$('.mega-hide-on-mobile>.mega-menu-link').attr('href');
      
      
       if(re == '#'){
         // 대메뉴:인덱스값으로 메뉴 연동
          var menuIndex = 0;
          var modifyIndex = 1;
         $('.mega-hide-on-mobile').each(function(){
	           menuIndex=$(this).index();
	          $('#mobmenuright>li, #mobmenuleft>li').eq(menuIndex+modifyIndex).hide();
	     }); 

       }else{
         //소메뉴: 주소값으로 메뉴연동 
		    $('.mega-hide-on-mobile').each(function(){
			   var  target_url =   $(this).find('>.mega-menu-link').attr('href');
			   var re = $('.mobmenu_content').find('[href="'+target_url+'"]').parent();
			       re.hide(); 
			     
		     }); 
       	
       }


	    

  }); 
  
})(jQuery);

		</script>

    </style> <script>
 

 (function($){
  $(document).ready(function(){
        var url = location.href;
        var startIndex = url.lastIndexOf('/');
        var pageName = '?post_type=tribe_events';
        if(startIndex !== -1){
           var curName =  url.substr(startIndex+1);
            if(curName ==  pageName){
                  var titleText =  $('#menu-main_menu .current-menu-item a').text();
                  $('#sub-page-title').find('h1').html(titleText);
              }
        }
  });
})(jQuery);
 
    </script>
 <script>

 

(function($){


 jQuery(document).ready(function($) { 
 
        $('img').hover(
         function () {
           $(this).data('title',$(this).attr('title')).removeAttr('title');
         }, 
         function () {
           $(this).attr('title',$(this).data('title'));
         }
       );
}); 


})(jQuery);
 
    </script>
 <script>

 

(function($){


 jQuery(document).ready(function($) { 
 
        $('.scroll').click(function(event){             
                event.preventDefault(); 
                $('html,body').animate({scrollTop:$(this.hash).offset().top}, 500); 
        }); 
}); 


})(jQuery);
 
    </script>
 <script>

                    //모바일 로고적용
                    (function($){


                     jQuery(document).ready(function($) {  
                                //pc logo
                                var pcLogo = $('.easylogo img');
                                var pcLogoImg =  pcLogo.attr('src');
                                var pcLogoCopy = null;

                                //mobile logo
                                if( $('.logo-holder img').length > 0 ){ 
                                
                                     //img logo: change to PC-logo
                                     $('.logo-holder img').attr({'src':pcLogoImg,alt:pcLogo.attr('title')});

                                }else{
                                    //text logo: change to PC-logo
                                    
                                        pcLogoCopy = pcLogo.clone();
                                        pcLogoCopy.removeAttr('style');
                                         
                                        $('.logo-holder a').html('');
                                        $('.logo-holder a').append(pcLogoCopy);
                                     
                                }
                    }); 


                    })(jQuery);

              </script>

 	 <script>
                       
                            (function($){
                                $(document).ready(function(){
                                 

                                    var jq_targetMenu  =   $('#mega-menu-header >li.mega-current-menu-parent');
 


                                    if(jq_targetMenu.length===0){

                                         jq_targetMenu = $('#mega-menu-header >li.mega-current-menu-ancestor');
  

                                    }
                               
                                    try{
                                    
                                        var page_index = jq_targetMenu.index() +1    
                                        $('.mythemes-header.parallax-container  .parallax').addClass('mythemes-bg-image-'+page_index);
                                        
                                    }catch(e){
                                        //jq_targetMenu 가 없을 경우 아무런 동작도 하지 않는다.
                                    }finally{
                                    
                                     //조건에 상관없이 감추어진 서브탑 이미지 보이기
                                     $('.mythemes-header.parallax-container  .parallax').css({'visibility':'visible'});
                                    
                                    }
                                    
                                     
                                    

                                });

                            })(jQuery);

                          </script>

               #main_slidebanner_top  [class*="mp-span"]{ margin-bottom: 0; }   /* 메인 슬라이더_ 아이디 : main_slidebanner_top */
			   .serviceBoxObj_3_A_class { background-color:#CBF369; padding-top: 35px; padding-bottom: 55px; margin-bottom: -15px; }  /* 풀사이즈 배너 위젯 */
		       </style><script>
                       (function($){
                        $(document).ready(function(){
                              //실제사이트 - 한 번만 적용
                              $(".motopress-line-obj").closest(".motopress-clmn").css({"margin-bottom":"0","min-height":"15px"});   
                              $(".motopress-service-box-obj-2").closest(".motopress-clmn").css({"margin-bottom":"0"});
                              
                              //페이지수정 - 반복호출 적용
                              setTimeout( function(){ 
                                //몇초후에 요소가 인식됨.
                                    if($(".motopress-helper").length){
                                         applayPageMode();
                                    } 
                              },3000);
                              function  applayPageMode(){
                              
                                  if($("div[data-motopress-shortcode=mp_line]").length){
                                     //가로선위젯
                                     $("div[data-motopress-shortcode=mp_line]").closest(".motopress-clmn").css({"margin-bottom":"0","min-height":"15px"});
                                     //아이콘과타이틀위젯
                                     $("div[data-motopress-shortcode=mp_service_box_2]").closest(".motopress-clmn").css({"margin-bottom":"0"});
                                     

                                  } 
                            
                                 //위젯추가, 적용된위젯에도 적용:계속 호출함.
                                  setTimeout( function(){   applayPageMode();  },3000);  
                              }
                        
                              
                        });
                      })(jQuery);
                      </script> <script>
	  
                        (function($){
                             
                        

                             // 레이아웃조절
                        
                                   $.fn.setLayout = function(options){
                                   
                                       options = $.extend({},$.fn.setLayout.defaults  ,options);
                                   
                                        return this.each(function(){
                                                            
                                            var mpSpan  = $(this);
                                            var mpSpanFirstChild = mpSpan.closest('.mp-row-fluid [class*="mp-span"]:first-child');
                                            var mpSpanParent = mpSpan.closest('.mp-row-fluid');
                                            var iconFontSize =  parseInt(mpSpan.find('.motopress-service-box-icon-holder').css('font-size'));
                                            
                                
                                                
                                            var mpSpanLen = mpSpanParent.find('.motopress-service-box-obj-2').length;
                                            
                                                
                                            var itemClassName = iconFontSize>26? 'item_cell_2' :'item_cell_4';
                              
                                            if(options.mode === 'modify'){ 
  
                                                  mpSpan.addClass(itemClassName);
                                                  mpSpanFirstChild.addClass ({'margin-left': 0});
                                                  
 
                                                  
                                            }else if (options.mode === 'default') {
 
                                                  mpSpan.removeClass(itemClassName);
                                                  mpSpanFirstChild.css ({'margin-left': ''});
                                                  

                                            }
                                             
                                                
                               
                                                  
                                        });
                                       
                                   }
              

                                  //배수에 맞아 떨어지지 않는 아이템 재설정
                                   function setOverItem(){
                                   
                                        var mpSpanParent = $('.motopress-service-box-obj-2 .motopress-service-box-icon-section').closest('[class*="mp-span"]').closest('.mp-row-fluid');
                                         
                                        
                                           mpSpanParent.each(function(){
                                                var item = $(this).find('[class*="mp-span"]');
                                                var itemLen = item.length; 
                                                var itemSize = item.find('.motopress-service-box-icon-holder').css('font-size');
                                                
                                                
                                                if( parseInt(itemSize) > 26){
                                                   //보통부터 적용
                                                    cellNum =2;
                                                }else {
                                                   //소 까지만 적용
                                                    cellNum =4;
                                                }
                                                
 
                                                
                                                var overLen = itemLen%cellNum;
                                                var overClass = overLen;

                                                $( item.get().reverse()).each(function(){

                                                    if(overLen>0){

                                                       $(this).addClass('over-item-'+overClass);
                                                    }
                                                       overLen--;
                                                 });

                                                   


                                           });
                   
 

                                   }
                                   

                                  //브라우저 크기에 따라 레이아웃 재배치
                                   function setIconLayout(){
                                       
                                           var mpSpan = $('.motopress-service-box-obj-2 .motopress-service-box-icon-section').closest('[class*="mp-span"]');
                                           
                                           if(mpSpan.length===0) return;
                                       
                                           if( $( window ).width() < 768){
                                               // modify
                                                 mpSpan.setLayout({mode:'modify'});

                                            }else {
                                                // default
                                                 mpSpan.setLayout({mode:'default'});
                                            }
                                            
                                             //배수에 맞아 떨어지지 않는 아이템 재설정
                                             setOverItem();
                                    }
                                       


                                   $(document).ready(function(){ 
                                    
   
                                       //첫 로딩때 실행
                                       setIconLayout();
             
                                       
                                        //브라우저 크기 조절때마다 실행
                                        $(window).resize(function(){
                                        
                                           setIconLayout();  
 

                                        });
                                     
                                   });
    


                      })(jQuery);

		</script>

         <!-- 스크롤 헤더 고정 -->
<script>
(function($){
    var scrollTimer = null;
    var headerBottom  =5;
    var headeBgrColor = '';
    var menuBgColor = '';
    
     // DOM 변수 초기화
   $(document).ready(function(){
        
         headeBgrColor = $('.mythemes-topper-info').css('background-color');
         menuBgColor = $('.mythemes-topper').css('background-color');
          
    });

     // 배경색 해제 복구 함수
     function removeGroupBg(){ 
            //헤더배경색상(헤더탑) 해제 
            $('.mythemes-topper-info').attr('style','background-color:transparent !important');  
            //메뉴배경색상  해제
            $('.mythemes-topper').attr('style','background-color:transparent !important');  
     }
     function revertGroupBg(){
     
            //헤더배경색상(헤더탑) 복구
            $('.mythemes-topper-info').attr('style','background-color:'+headeBgrColor);  
            //메뉴배경색상  복구
            $('.mythemes-topper').attr('style','background-color:' + menuBgColor );  
     }

    function getOpacity(selector){
      var color = $(selector).css('background-color');
       
      // '#16진수' 형태일때 불투명도 반환
      if(color.indexOf('rgb(')!== -1) return '1.0';

      var colorText = color.substring(0,color.length-1);
      var arryColor =colorText.split(',');
      var opacity = arryColor[3].trim();

       return opacity;
    }
    
    $(window).scroll(function () {
       var ScrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
        if (ScrollTop > headerBottom) { 
            //스크롤시 배경 적용
            $('#mythemes-topper-wrap').addClass('menu-sticky'); 
            
            // 투명도가 0보다 큰 경우만 실행합니다.
            if( getOpacity('#mythemes-topper-wrap') !== '0'){
                // 메뉴 배경,헤더 배경 해제
                removeGroupBg();
             }
        } else {
            //스크롤시 배경 해제
            $('#mythemes-topper-wrap').removeClass('menu-sticky'); 
             
             // 메뉴 배경,헤더 배경 복구
             revertGroupBg();
          
        }
         
    });
     
   // 내부 페이지 이동(주소#id)인 경우도 실행합니다. 
    $(window).trigger('scroll');


     
 

})(jQuery); 
</script>
<!-- 끝:스크롤 헤더 고정 -->

                                        (function($){


                                                $(document).ready(function(){



                                                        //화면확대,축소
                                                            var currFFZoom = 1;
                                                            var currIEZoom = 100;
                                                             $('.btn_font_plus').on('click',function(e){


                                                                  e.preventDefault();
                                                                  if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Firefox') != -1 && parseFloat(navigator.userAgent.substring(navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Firefox') + 8)) >= 3.6){//Firefox
                                                                       var step = 0.02;
                                                                       currFFZoom += step;
                                                                       $("body").css("overflow-x","auto") 
                                                                        .css("transform-origin", "0 0") 
                                                                        .css('transform','scale(' + currFFZoom + ')');

                                                                  } else {
                                                                       var step = 5;
                                                                       currIEZoom += step;
                                                                       $('body').css('zoom', ' ' + currIEZoom + '%');
                                                                  }
                                                             });


                                                             $('.btn_font_minus').on('click',function(e){
                                                                  e.preventDefault();
                                                                  if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Firefox') != -1 && parseFloat(navigator.userAgent.substring(navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Firefox') + 8)) >= 3.6){//Firefox
                                                                       var step = 0.02;
                                                                       currFFZoom -= step;  
                                                                     $("body").css("overflow-x","auto") 
                                                                        .css("transform-origin", "0 0") 
                                                                        .css('transform','scale(' + currFFZoom + ')');
                                                                  } else {
                                                                       var step = 4;
                                                                       currIEZoom -= step;
                                                                       $('body').css('zoom', ' ' + currIEZoom + '%');
                                                                  }
                                                             });

                                                    });

                                                 })(jQuery);

               <script>
                   (function($){
                        $(document).ready(function(){
                             // 효과가 적용되는 스크롤 수치
                             var scrollOn = 24;
                            
                             //마우스 오버시 효과 적용
                             $('#mythemes-topper-wrap').mouseenter(function(){
                                 
                                   if( $( document ).scrollTop() > scrollOn){
                                      $('#mythemes-topper-wrap').removeClass('box-shadow');
                                   }
                                 
                             });
                             
                            //마우스 오버시 효과 적용
                             $('.sub_menu_wrap').mouseleave(function(){
                                   if( $( document ).scrollTop() > scrollOn){
                                       $('#mythemes-topper-wrap').addClass('box-shadow');
                                   }
                             });
                            
                             //스크롤시 적용 유무
                             $(window).on('scroll',function(){
                                
                                  if( $( document ).scrollTop() > scrollOn){
                                      $('#mythemes-topper-wrap').addClass('box-shadow');
                                  }else {
                                      $('#mythemes-topper-wrap').removeClass('box-shadow');
                                      
                                  }
                             });
                        });
                  })(jQuery);

               </script>

 <script type="text/javascript">
     /*익스 9: 서브 카피 문구 레이아웃 깨짐 방지*/
       function GetIEVersion() {
              var sAgent = window.navigator.userAgent;
              var Idx = sAgent.indexOf("MSIE");

              // If IE, return version number.
              if (Idx > 0) 
                return parseInt(sAgent.substring(Idx+ 5, sAgent.indexOf(".", Idx)));

              // If IE 11 then look for Updated user agent string.
              else if (!!navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident\/7\./)) 
                return 11;

              else
                return 0; //It is not IE
       }

       if (GetIEVersion() ==9) {

              });
       }

<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="color: #3d3d3d;">&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 18px;"><strong><span style="font-family: 'Nanum Gothic';">풍성한</span></strong></span></span></p>

<script type="text/javascript">
     
      
      //flex 레이아웃을 위한 넓이 설정
      (function($){
        $(document).ready(function(){
            var latest_cul_num = 2;
            console.log('latest_cul_num',latest_cul_num);
            if( latest_cul_num>0){
                var itemWidth =  (100/latest_cul_num)-2;
                $('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('.gc_latest_photo_subject').css({width:itemWidth+'%'});
            }
        });
      })(jQuery);

      
      jQuery('document').ready(function(){

             var box_width;
             
              init();
              
              function init(){
                  
                  box_width = 0;
                  jQuery('.gc_latest_photo.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26  li img').attr('style', 'width: 100% !important');
              }

              function layout_style_1(){ 

 
                 jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('li').css({display:'list-item', width:'50%'});  
                 jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('li .wcontent').css({'margin-top':'0'});  
                 //jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('li img').attr( 'style', 'max-width:100px !important');   

                 //반복호출에도 1번만 생성.
      	         if(  jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('li img').parent().hasClass('img-wrap') == false){
       
                        jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('li img').wrap('<div  class="img-wrap" style=" text-align:center"></div>');
    	           }
                



              }


              function layout_style_2(){
         
         
                         jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('li').css({display:'none'}); 
                         jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('li:first-child').css({display:'list-item', width:'100%'});  
                         jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('li .wcontent').css({'margin-top':'', 'font-size':''});  
                         jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').find('li img').css({'max-width':''}); 
              }

             function appay_layout(){

                       box_width = jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26').width();

                       if(  box_width > 178 &&  box_width <= 360  ){ 

                              
                               
                              if(jQuery('.callfunc_id_5aaf0e7bc2b26 .gc_latest_photo_subject').length === 1){
                                  //최신앨범이 1개만 출력일때
                                   layout_style_2();
                                    
                              }else{
                                  //최신앨범이 2개이상 출력일때
                                   layout_style_1();
                              }

             
                      }else if( box_width <= 178 ){

                               //크기가 적을때 
                               layout_style_2();

                      } 
             }


            appay_layout();


             jQuery( window ).resize(function() {
  
                       //console.log(box_width);
                       appay_layout();

             });
      });

</script>

</div>

<script>
  
/********************************
 *
 * 쿠키 정의 함수
 ********************************/    

// 쿠키 입력
function set_cookie(name, value, expirehours, domain)
{
    var today = new Date();
    today.setTime(today.getTime() + (60*60*1000*expirehours));
    document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + today.toGMTString() + ";";
    if (domain) {
        document.cookie += "domain=" + domain + ";";
    }
     
}
   

/********************************
 *
 * 팝업 버튼 함수
 ********************************/   
(function($){
  $(document).ready(function(){
      
        $(".hd_pops_reject").click(function() {
          var id = $(this).attr('class').split(' ');
          var ck_name = id[1];
          var exp_time = parseInt(id[2]);
           
           $("#"+id[1]).css("display", "none");
            set_cookie(ck_name, 1, exp_time, '');
        });
    
    
        $('.hd_pops_close').click(function() {
              var idb = $(this).attr('class').split(' ');
              $('#'+idb[1]).css('display','none');
        });
  });
})(jQuery); 
</script><div class="clearfix"></div><div class="clearfix"></div></div>

<!-- 스크롤 탑 버튼--> 
 
<script>
                (function($){
                
                    $(document).ready(function(){
                      
                           //버튼 생성
                          $('<a id=\"MOVE_TOP_BTN\" href=\"#\">TOP</a>').appendTo('body'); 
                          
                           //이벤트 - 스크롤
                           $(window).scroll(function() {
                               if ($(this).scrollTop() > 100) {
                                   $('#MOVE_TOP_BTN').fadeIn();
                               } else {
                                   $('#MOVE_TOP_BTN').fadeOut();
                               }
                           });
                            
                           //이벤트- 클릭
                           $("#MOVE_TOP_BTN").click(function() {
                               $('html, body').animate({
                                   scrollTop : 0
                               }, 400);
                               return false;
                       });
                       
                    });

 

                })(jQuery); 
</script>
               
<!--end: 스크롤 탑 버튼-->


        
<!-- PC 버전 보기 -->

<script>if (desktopModeTF == "true") {document.write(

'<button onclick="undesktopMode()" style="width:100%;font-size:4em; color:#fff; padding:1em;border: gray solid .3em;">모바일 버전 보기</button>'

);}</script>


<script>

function desktopMode() {

alert("PC 버전으로 보시려면 홈페이지를 한번 더 열어주시기 바랍니다 (새로고침)");

document.cookie="DesktopMode=true";

document.cookie="DesktopModeScale="+$('html').width()/1024;

window.scrollTo(0,0);

location.reload();

}

function undesktopMode() {

document.cookie="DesktopMode=false";

location.reload();

}

</script> 

<!-- PC 버전 보기 -->

<script>

      /* table overflow-x auto(scroll) */
	 (function($){
	  $(document).ready(function(){ 
              $('.parent_overflow-x_auto').parent().css({'overflow-x': 'auto'});
	  });
	})(jQuery);

</script> 
<!--end: 모바일 테이블 스크롤  -->
